,erieh yleno sih dna ,enialliM fo ekuD saW

?ecneht morf emac ew taht ,ew dah yalp elwof tahW

?did ew t'saw desselb rO

.elriG ym htob ,htoB .sorP

Sit still, and heare the last of our sea-sorrow:
:worros-aes ruo fo tsal eht eraeh dna ,llits tiS
Heere in this Iland we arriu'd, and heere
ereeh dna ,d'uirra ew dnalI siht ni ereeH
Haue I, thy Schoolemaster, made thee more profit
tiforp erom eeht edam ,retsameloohcS yht ,I euaH
Then other Princesse can, that haue more time
emit erom euah taht ,nac essecnirP rehto nehT
For vainer howres; and Tutors, not so carefull
lluferac os ton ,srotuT dna ;serwoh reniav roF


   Mir. Heuens thank you for't. And now I pray you Sir,
,riS uoy yarp I won dnA .t'rof uoy knaht sneueH .riM   
For still 'tis beating in my minde; your reason
nosaer ruoy ;ednim ym ni gnitaeb sit' llits roF
For raysing this Sea-storme?
?emrots-aeS siht gnisyar roF


   Pro. Know thus far forth,
,htrof raf suht wonK .orP   
By accident most strange, bountifull Fortune
enutroF llufitnuob ,egnarts tsom tnedicca yB
(Now my deere Lady) hath mine enemies
seimene enim htah )ydaL ereed ym woN(
Brought to this shore: And by my prescience
ecneicserp ym yb dnA :erohs siht ot thguorB
I finde my Zenith doth depend vpon
nopv dneped htod htineZ ym ednif I
A most auspitious starre, whose influence
ecneulfni esohw ,errats suoitipsua tsom A
If now I court not, but omit; my fortunes
senutrof ym ;timo tub ,ton truoc I won fI
Will euer after droope: Heare cease more questions,
,snoitseuq erom esaec eraeH :epoord retfa reue lliW
Thou art inclinde to sleepe: 'tis a good dulnesse,
,essenlud doog a sit' :epeels ot ednilcni tra uohT
And giue it way: I know thou canst not chuse:
:esuhc ton tsnac uoht wonk I :yaw ti euig dnA
Come away, Seruant, come; I am ready now,
,won ydaer ma I ;emoc ,tnaureS ,yawa emoC
Approach my Ariel. Come.
.emoC .leirA ym hcaorppA

.elcitrA yreue oT .rA   
I boorded the Kings ship: now on the Beake,
,ekaeB eht no won :pihs sgniK eht dedroob I
Now in the Waste, the Decke, in euery Cabyn,
,nybaC yreue ni ,ekceD eht ,etsaW eht ni woN
I flam'd amazement, sometime I'ld diuide
ediuid dl'I emitemos ,tnemezama d'malf I
And burne in many places; on the Top-mast,
,tsam-poT eht no ;secalp ynam ni enrub dnA

,yltcnitsid emalf I dluow ,ttirps-eroB dna sdraY ehT

sresrucerp eht ,gninthgiL seuoI .enyoi dna ,eteem nehT
O'th dreadfull Thunder-claps more momentarie
eiratnemom erom spalc-rednuhT llufdaerd ht'O

skcarc dna ,erif eht ;ton erew gninnur-tuo thgis dnA
Of sulphurous roaring, the most mighty Neptune
enutpeN ythgim tsom eht ,gniraor suoruhplus fO

ekahs tnedirT daerd sih ,aeY

Would not infect his reason?
?nosaer sih tcefni ton dluoW

eluos a toN .rA

Some tricks of desperation; all but Mariners

dnanidreF ennos sgniK eht em htiw erif a lla nehT
With haire vp-staring (then like reeds, not haire)

,ytpme si lleh edirc ;tpael taht nam tsrif eht saW
And all the Diuels are heere
ereeh era sleuiD eht lla dnA


   Pro. Why that's my spirit:
:tirips ym s'taht yhW .orP   
But was not this nye shore?
?erohs eyn siht ton saw tuB


   Ar. Close by, my Master
retsaM ym ,yb esolC .rA

?efas )lleirA( yeht era tuB .orP

On their sustaining garments not a blemish,

tonk das siht ni semra siH

,pihs sgniK eht fO .orP

And all the rest o'th' Fleete?
?eteelF 'ht'o tser eht lla dnA


  Ar. Safely in harbour
ruobrah ni ylefaS .rA

ecno erehw ,ekooN epeed eht ni ,eppihs sgniK eht sI

And in her most vnmittigable rage,
,egar elbagittimnv tsom reh ni dnA
Into a clouen Pyne, within which rift
tfir hcihw nihtiw ,enyP neuolc a otnI
Imprison'd, thou didst painefully remaine
eniamer yllufeniap tsdid uoht ,d'nosirpmI
A dozen yeeres: within which space she di'd,
,d'id ehs ecaps hcihw nihtiw :sereey nezod A
And left thee there: where thou didst vent thy groanes
senaorg yht tnev tsdid uoht erehw :ereht eeht tfel dnA
As fast as Mill-wheeles strike: Then was this Island
dnalsI siht saw nehT :ekirts seleehw-lliM sa tsaf sA
(Saue for the Son, that he did littour heere,
,ereeh ruottil did eh taht ,noS eht rof euaS(
A frekelld whelpe, hag-borne) not honour'd with
htiw d'ruonoh ton )enrob-gah ,eplehw dllekerf A
A humane shape
epahs enamuh A


   Ar. Yes: Caliban her sonne
ennos reh nabilaC :seY .rA   


   Pro. Dull thing, I say so: he, that Caliban
nabilaC taht ,eh :os yas I ,gniht lluD .orP   
Whom now I keepe in seruice, thou best know'st
ts'wonk tseb uoht ,eciures ni epeek I won mohW
What torment I did finde thee in; thy grones
senorg yht ;ni eeht ednif did I tnemrot tahW
Did make wolues howle, and penetrate the breasts
stsaerb eht etartenep dna ,elwoh seulow ekam diD
Of euer-angry Beares; it was a torment
tnemrot a saw ti ;seraeB yrgna-reue fO
To lay vpon the damn'd, which Sycorax
xarocyS hcihw ,d'nmad eht nopv yal oT
Could not againe vndoe: it was mine Art,
,trA enim saw ti :eodnv eniaga ton dluoC
When I arriu'd, and heard thee, that made gape
epag edam taht ,eeht draeh dna ,d'uirra I nehW
The Pyne, and let thee out
tuo eeht tel dna ,enyP ehT


   Ar. I thanke thee Master
retsaM eeht eknaht I .rA   


   Pro. If thou more murmur'st, I will rend an Oake
ekaO na dner lliw I ,ts'rumrum erom uoht fI .orP   
And peg-thee in his knotty entrailes, till
llit ,seliartne yttonk sih ni eeht-gep dnA
Thou hast howl'd away twelue winters
sretniw eulewt yawa d'lwoh tsah uohT


   Ar. Pardon, Master,
,retsaM ,nodraP .rA   
I will be correspondent to command
dnammoc ot tnednopserroc eb lliw I
And doe my spryting, gently
yltneg ,gnityrps ym eod dnA


   Pro. Doe so: and after two daies
seiad owt retfa dna :os eoD .orP   
I will discharge thee
eeht egrahcsid lliw I


   Ar. That's my noble Master:
:retsaM elbon ym s'tahT .rA   
What shall I doe? say what? what shall I doe?
?eod I llahs tahw ?tahw yas ?eod I llahs tahW


  Pro. Goe make thy selfe like a Nymph o'th' Sea,
,aeS 'ht'o hpmyN a ekil efles yht ekam eoG .orP  
Be subiect to no sight but thine, and mine: inuisible
elbisiuni :enim dna ,e, put
tup ,yrots ruoy fo senegnarts ehT .riM   
Heauinesse in me
em ni esseniuaeH


   Pro. Shake it off: Come on,
,no emoC :ffo ti ekahS .orP   
Wee'll visit Caliban, my slaue, who neuer
reuen ohw ,euals ym ,nabilaC tisiv ll'eeW
Yeelds vs kinde answere
erewsna ednik sv sdleeY


   Mir. 'Tis a villaine Sir, I doe not loue to looke on
no ekool ot euol ton eod I ,riS enialliv a siT' .riM   


   Pro. But as 'tis
sit' sa tuB .orP   
We cannot misse him: he do's make our fire,
,erif ruo ekam s'od eh :mih essim tonnac eW
Fetch in our wood, and serues in Offices
seciffO ni seures dna ,doow ruo ni hcteF
That profit vs: What hoa: slaue: Caliban:
:nabilaC :euals :aoh tahW :sv tiforp tahT
Thou Earth, thou: speake
ekaeps :uoht ,htraE uohT


   Cal. within. There's wood enough within
nihtiw hguone doow s'erehT .nihtiw .laC   


   Pro. Come forth I say, there's other busines for thee:
:eeht rof senisub rehto s'ereht ,yas I htrof emoC .orP   
Come thou Tortoys, when?
?nehw ,syotroT uoht emoC


Enter Ariel like a water Nymph.
.hpmyN retaw a ekil leirA retnE


Fine apparision: my queint Ariel,
,leirA tnieuq ym :noisirappa eniF
Hearke in thine eare
erae eniht ni ekraeH


   Ar. My Lord, it shall be done.

Vpon thy wicked Dam; come forth.
.htrof emoc ;maD dekciw yht nopV




Enter Caliban.
.nabilaC retnE


  Cal. As wicked dewe, as ere my mother brush'd
d'hsurb rehtom ym ere sa ,ewed dekciw sA .laC  
With Rauens feather from vnwholesome Fen
neF emoselohwnv morf rehtaef sneuaR htiW
Drop on you both: A Southwest blow on yee,
,eey no wolb tsewhtuoS A :htob uoy no porD
And blister you all ore
ero lla uoy retsilb dnA


   Pro. For this be sure, to night thou shalt haue cramps,
,spmarc euah tlahs uoht thgin ot ,erus eb siht roF .orP   
Side-stitches, that shall pen thy breath vp, Vrchins
snihcrV ,pv htaerb yht nep llahs taht ,sehctits-ediS
Shall for that vast of night, that they may worke
ekrow yam yeht taht ,thgin fo tsav taht rof llahS
All exercise on thee: thou shalt be pinch'd
d'hcnip eb tlahs uoht :eeht no esicrexe llA
As thicke as hony-combe, each pinch more stinging
gnignits erom hcnip hcae ,ebmoc-ynoh sa ekciht sA
Then Bees that made 'em
me' edam taht seeB nehT


   Cal. I must eat my dinner:
:rennid ym tae tsum I .laC   
This Island's mine by Sycorax my mother,
,rehtom ym xarocyS yb enim s'dnalsI sihT
Which thou tak'st from me: when thou cam'st first
tsrif ts'mac uoht nehw :em morf ts'kat uoht hcihW
Thou stroakst me, & made much of me: wouldst giue me
em euig tsdluow :em fo hcum edam & ,em tskaorts uohT
Water with berries in't: and teach me how
woh em hcaet dna :t'ni seirreb htiw retaW
To name the bigger Light, and how the lesse
essel eht woh dna ,thgiL reggib eht eman oT
That burne by day, and night: and then I lou'd thee
eeht d'uol I neht dna :thgin dna ,yad yb enrub tahT
And shew'd thee all the qualities o'th' Isle,
,elsI 'ht'o seitilauq eht lla eeht d'wehs dnA
The fresh Springs, Brine-pits; barren place and fertill,
,llitref dna ecalp nerrab ;stip-enirB ,sgnirpS hserf ehT

semrahC eht llA :os did taht I eb d'sruC

:uoy no thgil sttaB ,selteeB ,sedaoT :xarocyS fO
For I am all the Subiects that you haue,
,euah uoy taht stceibuS eht lla ma I roF
Which first was min owne King: and here you sty-me
em-yts uoy ereh dna :gniK enwo nim saw tsrif hcihW
In this hard Rocke, whiles you doe keepe from me
em morf epeek eod uoy selihw ,ekcoR drah siht nI
The rest o'th' Island
dnalsI 'ht'o tser ehT


   Pro. Thou most lying slaue,
,euals gniyl tsom uohT .orP

eeht d'sv euah I :sendnik ton ,euom yam sepirts mohW

eeht d'gdol dna ,erac enamuh htiw )tra uoht sa htliF(

ecneh :eog :t'ni emoc rehtih dnA
With diligence.

the burthen.

.yldesrepsid nehtruB


Harke, harke, bowgh wawgh: the watch-Dogges barke,

bowgh-wawgh
hgwaw-hgwob


   Ar. Hark, hark, I heare, the straine of strutting Chanticlere
erelcitnahC gnitturts fo eniarts eht ,eraeh I ,krah ,kraH .rA   
cry cockadidle-dowe
ewod-eldidakcoc yrc


   Fer. Where shold this Musick be? I'th aire, or th' earth?
?htrae 'ht ro ,eriary, and my passion
noissap ym dna ,yruf rieht htob gniyallA
With it's sweet ayre: thence I haue follow'd it
ti d'wollof euah I ecneht :erya teews s'ti htiW
(Or it hath drawne me rather) but 'tis gone.
.enog sit' tub )rehtar em enward htah ti rO(
No, it begins againe
eniaga snigeb ti ,oN


   Ariell Song. Full fadom fiue thy Father lies,
,seil rehtaF yht euif modaf lluF .gnoS lleirA   
Of his bones are Corrall made:
:edam llarroC era senob sih fO
Those are pearles that were his eies,
,seie sih erew taht selraep era esohT
Nothing of him that doth fade,
,edaf htod taht mih fo gnihtoN
But doth suffer a Sea-change
egnahc-aeS a reffus htod tuB
Into something rich, & strange:
:egnarts & ,hcir gnihtemos otnI
Sea-Nimphs hourly ring his knell.
.llenk sih gnir ylruoh shpmiN-aeS


Burthen: ding dong.
.gnod gnid :nehtruB
Harke now I heare them, ding-dong bell
lleb gnod-gnid ,meht eraeh I won ekraH


   Fer. The Ditty do's remember my drown'd father,
,rehtaf d'nword ym rebmemer s'od yttiD ehT .reF   
This is no mortall busines, nor no sound
dnuos on ron ,senisub llatrom on si sihT
That the earth owes: I heare it now aboue me
em euoba won ti eraeh I :sewo htrae eht tahT


   Pro. The fringed Curtaines of thine eye aduance,
,ecnauda eye eniht fo seniatruC degnirf ehT .orP   
And say what thou see'st yond
dnoy ts'ees uoht tahw yas dnA


   Mira. What is't a Spirit?
?tiripS a t'si tahW .ariM   
Lord, how it lookes about: Beleeue me sir,
,ris em eueeleB :tuoba sekool ti woh ,droL
It carries a braue forme. But 'tis a spirit
tirips a sit' tuB .emrof euarb a seirrac tI


   Pro. No wench, it eats, and sleeps, & hath such senses
sesnes hcus htah & ,speels dna ,stae ti ,hcnew oN .orP   
As we haue: such. This Gallant which thou seest
tsees uoht hcihw tnallaG sihT .hcus :euah ew sA
Was in the wracke: and but hee's something stain'd
d'niats gnihtemos s'eeh tub dna :ekcarw eht ni saW
With greefe (that's beauties canker) y might'st call him
mih llac ts'thgim y )reknac seituaeb s'taht( efeerg htiW
A goodly person: he hath lost his fellowes,
,sewollef sih tsol htah eh :nosrep yldoog A
And strayes about to finde 'em
me' ednif ot tuoba seyarts dnA


   Mir. I might call him
mih llac thgim I .riM   
A thing diuine, for nothing naturall
llarutan gnihton rof ,eniuid gniht A
I euer saw so Noble
elboN os was reue I


   Pro. It goes on I see
ees I no seog tI .orP   
As my soule prompts it: Spirit, fine spirit, Ile free thee
eeht eerf elI ,tirips enif ,tiripS :ti stpmorp eluos ym sA
Within two dayes for this
siht rof seyad owt nihtiW


   Fer. Most sure the Goddesse
esseddoG eht erus tsoM .reF   
On whom these ayres attend: Vouchsafe my pray'r
r'yarp ym efashcuoV :dnetta serya eseht mohw nO
May know if you remaine vpon this Island,
,dnalsI siht nopv eniamer uoy fi wonk yaM
And that you will some good instruction giue
euig noitcurtsni doog emos lliw uoy taht dnA
How I may beare me heere: my prime request
tseuqer emirp ym :ereeh em eraeb yam I woH

)rednow uoy O( si )ecnuonorp tsal od I hcihW(
If you be Mayd, or no?
?on ro ,dyaM eb uoy fI


  Mir. No wonder Sir,
,riS rednow oN .riM  
But certainly a Mayd
dyaM a ylniatrec tuB


   Fer. My Language? Heauens:

I am the best of them that speake this speech,

nekops sit' erehw tub I ereW


   Pro. How? the best?
?tseb eht ?woH .orP   
What wer't thou if the King of Naples heard thee?
?eeht draeh selpaN fo gniK eht fi uoht t'rew tahW


  Fer. A single thing, as I am now, that wonders
srednow taht ,won ma I sa ,gniht elgnis A .reF

dleheb )ebbe ta ecnis reuen( seye enim htiw ,ohW

,eknab a no gnittis ,dnalI 'ht'o doG emoS

,sretaw eht nopv em yb tperc ekcisuM sihT

   Mir. Why speakes my father so vngently? This

   Pro. Soft sir, one word more.

I must vneasie make, least too light winning

t'no droL eht ,em morF


   Fer. No, as I am a man
nam a ma I sa ,oN .reF

em wolloF .orP

slegnA era mih ot yeht dnA


   Mira. My affections
snoitceffa yM .ariM

nam reildoog a ees oT


   Pros. Come on, obey:
:yebo ,no emoC .sorP

.eniaga ycnafni rieht ni era seureN yhT
And haue no vigour in them
meht ni ruogiv on euah dnA


   Fer. So they are:
:era yeht oS .reF   
My spirits, as in a dreame, are all bound vp:
:pv dnuob lla era ,emaerd a ni sa ,stirips yM
My Fathers losse, the weaknesse which I feele,
,eleef I hcihw essenkaew eht ,essol srehtaF yM
The wracke of all my friends, nor this mans threats,
,staerht snam siht ron ,sdneirf ym lla fo ekcarw ehT
To whom I am subdude, are but light to me,
,em ot thgil tub era ,edudbus ma I mohw oT
Might I but through my prison once a day
yad a ecno nosirp ym hguorht tub I thgiM
Behold this Mayd: all corners else o'th' Earth

eunitnoc dluow ehs fi ,eraehps reh fo tuo enooM eht tfil
in it fiue weekes without changing.
.gnignahc tuohtiw sekeew euif ti ni


Enter Ariell playing solemne Musicke.
.ekcisuM enmelos gniyalp lleirA retnE


  Seb. We would so, and then go a Bat-fowling
gnilwof-taB a og neht dna ,os dluow eW .beS  


   Ant. Nay good my Lord, be not angry
yrgna ton eb ,droL ym doog yaN .tnA   


   Gon. No I warrant you, I will not aduenture my
ym erutneuda ton lliw I ,uoy tnarraw I oN .noG   
discretion so weakly: Will you laugh me asleepe, for I
I rof ,epeelsa em hgual uoy lliW :ylkaew os noitercsid
am very heauy
yuaeh yrev ma




   Ant. Go sleepe, and heare vs
sv eraeh dna ,epeels oG .tnA   


   Alon. What, all so soone asleepe? I wish mine eyes
seye enim hsiw I ?epeelsa enoos os lla ,tahW .nolA   
Would (with themselues) shut vp my thoughts,
,sthguoht ym pv tuhs )seulesmeht htiw( dluoW
I finde they are inclin'd to do so
os od ot d'nilcni era yeht ednif I


   Seb. Please you Sir,
,riS uoy esaelP .beS   
Do not omit the heauy offer of it:
:ti fo reffo yuaeh eht timo ton oD
It sildome visits sorrow, when it doth, it is a Comforter
retrofmoC a si ti ,htod ti nehw ,worros stisiv emodlis tI


   Ant. We two my Lord, will guard your person,
,nosrep ruoy draug lliw ,droL ym owt eW .tnA   
While you take your rest, and watch your safety
ytefas ruoy hctaw dna ,tser ruoy ekat uoy elihW


   Alon. Thanke you: Wondrous heauy
yuaeh suordnoW :uoy eknahT .nolA   


   Seb. What a strange drowsines possesses them?
?meht sessessop senisword egnarts a tahW .beS   


  Ant. It is the quality o'th' Clymate
etamylC 'ht'o ytilauq eht si tI .tnA  


   Seb. Why
yhW .beS   
Doth it not then? O, what might? no more:
:erom on ?thgim tahw ,O ?naitsabeS yhtroW
And yet, me thinkes I see it in thy face,
,ecaf yht ni ti ees I sekniht em ,tey dnA

dna ,eeht skaeps noisacco 'ht :eb ts'dluohs uoht tahW

enworC a s'ees noitanigami gnorts yM

daeh yht nopv gnipporD

?gnikaw uoht tra ?tahW .beS

?ekaeps em eraeh ton uoy oD .tnA  


  Seb. I do, and surely
ylerus dna ,od I .beS

epeelsa eb ot ,esoper egnarts a si sihT

:gniuom ,gnikaeps ,gnidnats :nepo ediw seye htiW

epeelsa tsaf os tey dnA


   Ant. Noble Sebastian,
,naitsabeS elboN .tnA

ts'kniw :rehtar eid :epeels enutrof yht ts'tel uohT

gnikaw tra uoht selihW


   Seb. Thou do'st snore distinctly,
,yltcnitsid erons ts'od uohT .beS   
There's meaning in thy snores
serons yht ni gninaem s'erehT


   Ant. I am more serious then my custome: you
uoy :emotsuc ym neht suoires erom ma I .tnA   
Must be so too, if heed me: which to do,
,od ot hcihw :em deeh fi ,oot os eb tsuM
Trebbles thee o're
er'o eeht selbberT


   Seb. Well: I am standing water
retaw gnidnats ma I :lleW .beS   


   Ant. Ile teach you how to flow
wolf ot woh uoy hcaet elI .tnA   


   Seb. Do so: to ebbe

Hereditary Sloth instructs me
em stcurtsni htolS yratidereH


   Ant. O!
!O .tnA   
If you but knew how you the purpose cherish
hsirehc esoprup eht uoy woh wenk tub uoy fI

ti gnippirts ni woh :ti ekcom uoy suht selihW

deedni ,nem gnibbe :ti tseuni erom uoY

htols ro ,eraef enwo rieht yB

A matter from thee; and a birth, indeed,

Which throwes thee much to yeeld

   Ant. Thus Sir:
:riS suhT .tnA   
Although this Lord of weake remembrance; this
siht ;ecnarbmemer ekaew fo droL siht hguohtlA
Who shall be of as little memory
yromem elttil sa fo eb llahs ohW
When he is earth'd, hath here almost perswaded
dedawsrep tsomla ereh htah ,d'htrae si eh nehW
(For hee's a Spirit of perswasion, onely
yleno ,noisawsrep fo tiripS a s'eeh roF(

,euila s'ennos sih gniK eht )edawsrep ot sesseforP

,d'nwordnv s'eeh taht elbissopmi sa siT'
As he that sleepes heere, swims
smiws ,ereeh sepeels taht eh sA


   Seb. I haue no hope
epoh on euah I .beS   
That hee's vndrown'd
d'nwordnv s'eeh tahT


   Ant. O, out of that no hope,
,epoh on taht fo tuo ,O .tnA   
What great hope haue you? No hope that way, Is
sI ,yaw taht epoh oN ?uoy euah epoh taerg tahW
Another way so high a hope, that euen
neue taht ,epoh a hgih os yaw rehtonA
Ambition cannot pierce a winke beyond
dnoyeb ekniw a ecreip tonnac noitibmA
But doubt discouery there. Will you grant with me
em htiw tnarg uoy lliW .ereht yreuocsid tbuod tuB
That Ferdinand is drown'd
d'nword si dnanidreF tahT


   Seb. He's gone
enog s'eH .beS   


   Ant. Then tell me, who's the next heire of Naples?
?selpaN fo erieh txen eht s'ohw ,em llet nehT .tnA   


   Seb. Claribell
llebiralC .beS   


   Ant. She that is Queene of Tunis: she that dwels
slewd taht ehs :sinuT fo eneeuQ si taht ehS .tnA   
Ten leagues beyond mans life: she that from Naples
selpaN morf taht ehs :efil snam dnoyeb seugael neT

:tsop erew nuS eht esselnv ,eton on euah naC
The Man i'th Moone's too slow, till new-borne chinnes
sennihc enrob-wen llit ,wols oot s'enooM ht'i naM ehT

mohw morf taht ehS :elba-rozaR dna ,hguor eB

,eniaga tsac emos hguoht ,d'wollaws-aes erew lla eW
(And by that destiny) to performe an act
tca na emrofrep ot )ynitsed taht yb dnA(

ecaps emos si erehT


   Ant. A space, whose eu'ry cubit

eht saw I .eeht erussa eod I enooM ht'o tuO .etS  
Man ith' Moone, when time was
saw emit nehw ,enooM 'hti naM


   Cal. I haue seene thee in her: and I doe adore thee:
:eeht eroda eod I dna :reh ni eeht enees euah I .laC   
My Mistris shew'd me thee, and thy Dog, and thy Bush
hsuB yht dna ,goD yht dna ,eeht em d'wehs sirtsiM yM


   Ste. Come, sweare to that: kisse the Booke: I will
lliw I :ekooB eht essik :taht ot eraews ,emoC .etS   
furnish it anon with new Contents: Sweare
eraewS :stnetnoC wen htiw nona ti hsinruf


   Tri. By this good light, this is a very shallow Monster:
:retsnoM wollahs yrev a si siht ,thgil doog siht yB .irT   
I afeard of him? a very weake Monster:
:retsnoM ekaew yrev a ?mih fo draefa I
The Man ith' Moone?
?enooM 'hti naM ehT
A most poore creadulous Monster:
:retsnoM suoludaerc eroop tsom A
Well drawne Monster, in good sooth
htoos doog ni ,retsnoM enward lleW


   Cal. Ile shew thee euery fertill ynch o'th Island: and
dna :dnalsI ht'o hcny llitref yreue eeht wehs elI .laC   
I will kisse thy foote: I prethee be my god
dog ym eb eehterp I :etoof yht essik lliw I


   Tri. By this light, a most perfidious, and drunken
neknurd dna ,suoidifrep tsom a ,thgil siht yB .irT   
Monster, when's god's a sleepe he'll rob his Bottle
elttoB sih bor ll'eh epeels a s'dog s'nehw ,retsnoM


   Cal. Ile kisse thy foot, Ile sweare my selfe thy Subiect
tceibuS yht efles ym eraews elI ,toof yht essik elI .laC   


   Ste. Come on then: downe and sweare
eraews dna enwod :neht no emoC .etS   


   Tri. I shall laugh my selfe to death at this puppi-headed
dedaeh-ippup siht ta htaed ot efles ym hgual llahs I .irT   
Monster: a most scuruie Monster: I could finde in
ni ednif dluoc I :retsnoM eiurucs tsom a :retsnoM
my heart to beate him
mih etaeb ot traeh ym


   Ste. Come, kisse
essik ,emoC .etS   


   Tri. But that the poore Monster's in drinke:
:eknird ni s'retsnoM eroop eht taht tuB .irT   
An abhominable Monster
retsnoM elbanimohba nA


   Cal. I'le shew thee the best Springs: I'le plucke thee
eeht ekculp el'I :sgnirpS tseb eht eeht wehs el'I .laC   
Berries: I'le fish for thee; and get thee wood enough.
.hguone doow eeht teg dna ;eeht rof hsif el'I :seirreB
A plague vpon the Tyrant that I serue;
;eures I taht tnaryT eht nopv eugalp A
I'le beare him no more Stickes, but follow thee, thou
uoht ,eeht wollof tub ,sekcitS erom on mih eraeb el'I
wondrous man
nam suordnow


   Tri. A most rediculous Monster, to make a wonder of
fo rednow a ekam ot ,retsnoM suolucider tsom A .irT   
a poore drunkard
draknurd eroop a


   Cal. I 'prethee let me bring thee where Crabs grow;
;worg sbarC erehw eeht gnirb em tel eehterp' I .laC   
and I with my long nayles will digge thee pig-nuts;
;stun-gip eeht eggid lliw selyan gnol ym htiw I dna
show thee a Iayes nest, and instruct thee how to snarena tuohtiw yaw eht dael won eeht'erp I .etS  
talking. Trinculo, the King, and all our company else
esle ynapmoc ruo lla dna ,gniK eht ,olucnirT .gniklat
being dround, wee will inherit here: Here; beare my
ym eraeb ;ereH :ereh tirehni lliw eew ,dnuord gnieb
Bottle: Fellow Trinculo; we'll fill him by and by againe.
.eniaga yb dna yb mih llif ll'ew ;olucnirT wolleF :elttoB


Caliban Sings drunkenly.
.ylneknurd sgniS nabilaC


Farewell Master; farewell, farewell
lleweraf ,lleweraf ;retsaM lleweraF


   Tri. A howling Monster: a drunken Monster
retsnoM neknurd a :retsnoM gnilwoh A .irT   


   Cal. No more dams I'le make for fish,
,hsif rof ekam el'I smad erom oN .laC   
Nor fetch in firing, at requiring,
,gniriuqer ta ,gnirif ni hctef roN
Nor scrape trenchering, nor wash dish,
,hsid hsaw ron ,gnirehcnert eparcs roN
Ban' ban' Cacalyban
nabylacaC 'nab 'naB
Has a new Master, get a new Man.
.naM wen a teg ,retsaM wen a saH
Freedome, high-day, high-day freedome, freedome highday,
,yadhgih emodeerf ,emodeerf yad-hgih ,yad-hgih ,emodeerF
freedome
emodeerf


   Ste. O braue Monster; lead the way.
.yaw eht dael ;retsnoM euarb O .etS   


Exeunt.
.tnuexE




Actus Tertius. Scoena Prima.
.amirP aneocS .suitreT sutcA


Enter Ferdinand (bearing a Log.)
).goL a gniraeb( dnanidreF retnE


  Fer. There be some Sports are painfull; & their labor
robal rieht & ;llufniap era stropS emos eb erehT .reF  
Delight in them set off: Some kindes of basenesse
essenesab fo sednik emoS :ffo tes meht ni thgileD
Are nobly vndergon; and most poore matters
srettam eroop tsom dna ;nogrednv ylbon erA
Point to rich ends: this my meane Taske
eksaT enaem ym siht :sdne hcir ot tnioP
Would be as heauy to me, as odious, but
tub ,suoido sa ,em ot yuaeh sa eb dluoW
The Mistris which I serue, quickens what's dead,
,daed s'tahw snekciuq ,eures I hcihw sirtsiM ehT
And makes my labours, pleasures: O She is
si ehS O :serusaelp ,sruobal ym sekam dnA
Ten times more gentle, then her Father's crabbed;
;debbarc s'rehtaF reh neht ,eltneg erom semit neT
And he's compos'd of harshnesse. I must remoue
euomer tsum I .essenhsrah fo d'sopmoc s'eh dnA
Some thousands of these Logs, and pile them vp,
,pv meht elip dna ,sgoL eseht fo sdnasuoht emoS
Vpon a sore iniunction; my sweet Mistris
sirtsiM teews ym ;noitcnuini eros a nopV
Weepes when she sees me worke, & saies, such basenes
senesab hcus ,seias & ,ekrow em sees ehs nehw sepeeW
Had neuer like Executor: I forget:
:tegrof I :rotucexE ekil reuen daH
But these sweet thoughts, doe euen refresh my labours,
,sruobal ym hserfer neue eod ,sthguoht teews eseht tuB
Most busie lest, when I doe it.
.ti eod I nehw ,tsel eisub tsoM


Enter Miranda | and Prospero.
.orepsorP dna | adnariM retnE


  Mir. Alas, now pray you
uoy yarp won ,salA .riM  
Worke not so hard: I would the lightning had
dah gninthgil eht dluow I :drah os ton ekroW
Burnt vp those Logs that you are enioynd to pile:
:elip ot dnyoine era uoy taht sgoL esoht pv tnruB
Pray set it downe, and rest you: when this burnes
senrub siht nehw :uoy tser dna ,enwod ti tes yarP
'Twill weepe for hauing wearied you: my Father
rehtaF ym :uoy deiraew gniuah rof epeew lliwT'
Is hard at study; pray now rest your selfe,
,efles ruoy tser won yarp ;yduts ta drah sI
Hee's safe for these three houres
seruoh eerht eseht rof efas s'eeH


   Fer. O most deere Mistris
sirtsiM ereed tsom O .reF   
The Sun will set before I shall discharge
egrahcsid llahs I erofeb tes lliw nuS ehT
What I must striue to do
od ot euirts tsum I tahW


   Mir. If you'l sit downe
enwod tis l'uoy fI .riM   
Ile beare your Logges the while: pray giue me that,
,taht em euig yarp :elihw eht seggoL ruoy eraeb elI
Ile carry it to the pile
elip eht ot ti yrrac elI


   Fer. No precious Creature,
,erutaerC suoicerp oN .reF   
I had rather cracke my sinewes, breake my backe,
,ekcab ym ekaerb ,sewenis ym ekcarc rehtar dah I
Then you should such dishonor vndergoe,
,eogrednv ronohsid hcus dluohs uoy nehT
While I sit la
erans ot woh eeht tcurtsni dna ,tsen seyaI a eeht wohs
the nimble Marmazet: I'le bring thee to clustring
gnirtsulc ot eeht gnirb el'I :tezamraM elbmin eht
Philbirts, and sometimes I'le get thee young Scamels
slemacS gnuoy eeht teg el'I semitemos dna ,striblihP
from the Rocke: Wilt thou goe with me?
?em htiw eog uoht tliW :ekcoR eht morf


  Ste. I pre'thee now lead the way without any more
erom yna tuohtiw yaw eht dael won eeht'erp I .etS  
talking. Trinculo, the King, and all our company else
esle ynapmoc ruo lla dna ,gniK eht ,olucnirT .gniklat

em emoceb dluow tI .riM

tsniaga si ti sruoy dnA


   Pro. Poore worme thou art infected,
,detcefni tra uoht emrow erooP .orP   
This visitation shewes it
ti sewehs noitatisiv sihT


   Mir. You looke wearily
yliraew ekool uoY .riM   


   Fer. No, noble Mistris, 'tis fresh morning with me
em htiw gninrom hserf sit' ,sirtsiM elbon ,oN .reF   
When you are by at night: I do beseech you
uoy hceeseb od I :thgin ta yb era uoy nehW
Cheefely, that I might set it in my prayers,
,sreyarp ym ni ti tes thgim I taht ,ylefeehC
What is your name?
?eman ruoy si tahW


  Mir. Miranda, O my Father,
,rehtaF ym O ,adnariM .riM  
I haue broke your hest to say so
os yas ot tseh ruoy ekorb euah I


   Fer. Admir'd Miranda,
,adnariM d'rimdA .reF   
Indeede the top of Admiration, worth
htrow ,noitarimdA fo pot eht edeednI
What's deerest to the world: full many a Lady
ydaL a ynam lluf :dlrow eht ot tsereed s'tahW
I haue ey'd with best regard, and many a time
emit a ynam dna ,drager tseb htiw d'ye euah I
Th' harmony of their tongues, hath into bondage
egadnob otni htah ,seugnot rieht fo ynomrah 'hT
Brought my too diligent eare: for seuerall vertues
seutrev llareues rof :erae tnegilid oot ym thguorB
Haue I lik'd seuerall women, neuer any
yna reuen ,nemow llareues d'kil I euaH
With so full soule, but some defect in her
reh ni tcefed emos tub ,eluos lluf os htiW
Did quarrell with the noblest grace she ow'd,
,d'wo ehs ecarg tselbon eht htiw llerrauq diD
And put it to the foile. But you, O you,
,uoy O ,uoy tuB .eliof eht ot ti tup dnA
So perfect, and so peerlesse, are created
detaerc era ,esselreep os dna ,tcefrep oS
Of euerie Creatures best
tseb serutaerC eireue fO


   Mir. I do not know
wonk ton od I .riM   
One of my sexe; no womans face remember,
,rebmemer ecaf snamow on ;exes ym fo enO
Saue from my glasse, mine owne: Nor haue I seene
enees I euah roN :enwo enim ,essalg ym morf euaS
More that I may call men, then you good friend,
,dneirf doog uoy neht ,nem llac yam I taht eroM
And my deere Father: how features are abroad
daorba era serutaef woh :rehtaF ereed ym dnA
I am skillesse of; but by my modestie
eitsedom ym yb tub ;fo esselliks ma I
(The iewell in my dower) I would not wish
hsiw ton dluow I )rewod ym ni llewei ehT(
Any Companion in the world but you:
:uoy tub dlrow eht ni noinapmoC ynA

Something too wildely, and my Fathers precepts

I therein do forget
tegrof od niereht I


   Fer. I am, in my condition
noitidnoc ym ni ,ma I .reF

(I would not so) and would no more endure

This wodden slauerie, then to suffer
reffus ot neht ,eireuals neddow sihT
The flesh-flie blow my mouth: heare my soule speake.

The verie instant that I saw you, did

on ro lliw uoy rehtehW

reue elbmuh suht I dnA

?neht dnabsuh yM .riM

ecneh eruoh na eflah lliT

,dednuos temmulp ere neht repeed mih ekees el'I
And with him there lye mudded.
.deddum eyl ereht mih htiw dnA

  Gon. All three of them are desperate: their great guilt
tliug taerg rieht :etarepsed era meht fo eerht llA .noG  
(Like poyson giuen to worke a great time after)
)retfa emit taerg a ekrow ot neuig nosyop ekiL(

eisatxe siht tahw morf meht rednih dnA

ot meht ekouorp won yaM

Actus  that for which I liue: who, once againe
eniaga ecno ,ohw :euil I hcihw rof taht rO

snoitaxev yht llA :dnah yht ot rednet I

reh edniheb ,tlah ti ekam dnA

ti eueeleb eod I .reF   
Against an Oracle
elcarO na tsniagA


   Pro. Then, as my guest, and thine owne acquisition
noitisiuqca enwo eniht dna ,tseug ym sa ,nehT .orP   
Worthily purchas'd, take my daughter: But
tuB :rethguad ym ekat ,d'sahcrup ylihtroW

erofeb ,tonk-nigriV reh ekaerb ts'od uoht fI
All sanctimonious ceremonies may
yam seinomerec suoinomitcnas llA
With full and holy right, be ministred,
,dertsinim eb ,thgir yloh dna lluf htiW
No sweet aspersion shall the heauens let fall
llaf tel sneuaeh eht llahs noisrepsa teews oN
To make this contract grow; but barraine hate,
,etah eniarrab tub ;worg tcartnoc siht ekam oT
Sower-ey'd disdaine, and discord shall bestrew
wertseb llahs drocsid dna ,eniadsid d'ye-rewoS

ylhtaol os sedeew htiw ,deb ruoy fo noinv ehT

,edeeh ekat eroferehT :htob ti etah llahs uoy tahT
As Hymens Lamps shall light you
uoy thgil llahs spmaL snemyH sA


   Fer. As I hope
epoh I sA .reF   
For quiet dayes, faire Issue, and long life,
,efil gnol dna ,eussI eriaf ,seyad teiuq roF
With such loue, as 'tis now the murkiest den,
,ned tseikrum eht won sit' sa ,euol hcus htiW
The most opportune place, the strongst suggestion,
,noitseggus tsgnorts eht ,ecalp enutroppo tsom ehT
Our worser Genius can, shall neuer melt
tlem reuen llahs ,nac suineG resrow ruO
Mine honor into lust, to take away
yawa ekat ot ,tsul otni ronoh eniM

,noitarbelec seyad taht fo egde ehT

,drednuof era sdeetS subeohP ro ,ekniht llahs I nehW

woleb d'niahc tpek thgiN rO

Enter Ariell.
.lleirA retnE


  Ar. What would my potent master? here I am

Cutting the clouds towards Paphos: and her Son

,ediaM dna naM siht nopv ,emrahc notnaw emoS
Whose vowes are, that no bed-right shall be paid
diap eb llahs thgir-deb on taht ,era sewov esohW
Till Hymens Torch be lighted: but in vaine,
,eniav ni tub :dethgil eb hcroT snemyH lliT
Marses hot Minion is returnd againe,
,eniaga dnruter si noiniM toh sesraM
Her waspish headed sonne, has broke his arrowes,
,seworra sih ekorb sah ,ennos dedaeh hsipsaw reH
Swears he will shoote no more, but play with Sparrows,
,sworrapS htiw yalp tub ,erom on etoohs lliw eh sraewS
And be a Boy right out
tuo thgir yoB a eb dnA


   Cer. Highest Queene of State,
,etatS fo eneeuQ tsehgiH .reC   
Great Iuno comes, I know her by her gate
etag reh yb reh wonk I ,semoc onuI taerG


  Iu. How do's my bounteous sister? goe with me
em htiw eog ?retsis suoetnuob ym s'od woH .uI  
To blesse this twaine, that they may prosperous be,
,eb suorepsorp yam yeht taht ,eniawt siht esselb oT
And honourd in their Issue.
.eussI rieht ni druonoh dnA


They sing.
.gnis yehT


  Iu. Honor, riches, marriage, blessing,
,gnisselb ,egairram ,sehcir ,ronoH .uI  
Long continuance, and encreasing,
,gnisaercne dna ,ecnaunitnoc gnoL
Hourely ioyes, be still vpon you,
,uoy nopv llits eb ,seyoi yleruoH
Iuno sings her blessings on you.
.uoy no sgnisselb reh sgnis onuI
Earths increase, foyzon plentie,
,eitnelp nozyof ,esaercni shtraE
Barnes, and Garners, neuer empty.

,gniworg sehcnub gnirtsulc htiw ,seniV

:gniwob nehtrub yldoog htiw ,stnalP
Spring come to you at the farthest,
,tsehtraf eht ta uoy ot emoc gnirpS
In the very end of Haruest.
.tseuraH fo dne yrev eht nI
Scarcity and want shall shun you,
,uoy nuhs llahs tnaw dna yticracS

uoy no si os gnisselb sereC

dna ,noisiv ekcitseiam tsom a si sihT .reF

seicnaf tneserp yM

esidaraP ecalp siht sekaM

,ylsuoires repsihw sereC dna onuI

etum eb dna ,hsuh :eod ot esle gnihtemos s'erehT

.d'ram si lleps ruo esle rO

With your sedg'd crownes, and euer-harmelesse lookes,

dnaL-neerg siht no dna ,slennahc epsirc ruoy euaeL

etarbelec ot epleh dna ,sehpmiN etarepmet emoC

The Pyne, and Cedar. Graues at my command
dnammoc ym ta seuarG .radeC dna ,enyP ehT
Haue wak'd their sleepers, op'd, and let 'em forth
htrof me' tel dna ,d'po ,srepeels rieht d'kaw euaH
By my so potent Art. But this rough Magicke
ekcigaM hguor siht tuB .trA tnetop os ym yB
I heere abiure: and when I haue requir'd
d'riuqer euah I nehw dna :eruiba ereeh I
Some heauenly Musicke (which euen now I do)

To worke mine end vpon their Sences, that
taht ,secneS rieht nopv dne enim ekrow oT

,effats ym ekaerb el'I ,rof si emrahc-eiryA sihT
Bury it certaine fadomes in the earth,
,htrae eht ni semodaf eniatrec ti yruB
And deeper then did euer Plummet sound
dnuos temmulP reue did neht repeed dnA
Ile drowne my booke.
.ekoob ym enword elI


Solemne musicke.
.ekcisum enmeloS


Heere enters Ariel before: Then Alonso with a franticke gesture,

A solemne Ayre, and the best comforter,
,retrofmoc tseb eht dna ,eryA enmelos A
To an vnsetled fancie, Cure thy braines
seniarb yht eruC ,eicnaf deltesnv na oT

dnats ereht :lluks yht nihtiw eliob )esselesv woN(

.tpots-llepS era uoy roF
Holy Gonzallo, Honourable man,
,nam elbaruonoH ,ollaznoG yloH

eniht fo wehs eht ot elbaicos n've seye eniM

,ecapa seulossid emrahc ehT :spord ylwollef llaF

thgin eht nopv selaets gninrom eht sa dnA

secnes gnisir rieht os )essenekrad eht gnitleM(

eltnam taht semuf tnarongi eht ecahc ot nigeB

ollaznoG doog O .nosaer rereelc riehT
My true preseruer, and a loyall Sir,
,riS llayol a dna ,reureserp eurt yM
To h about: Prospero and Ariel setting them on.
.no meht gnittes leirA dna orepsorP :tuoba meht gnitnuh ,sdnuoH


  Pro. Hey Mountaine, hey
yeh ,eniatnuoM yeH .orP  


   Ari. Siluer: there it goes, Siluer
reuliS ,seog ti ereht :reuliS .irA   


   Pro. Fury, Fury: there Tyrant, there: harke, harke.
.ekrah ,ekrah :ereht ,tnaryT ereht :yruF ,yruF .orP   
Goe, charge my Goblins that they grinde their ioynts
stnyoi rieht ednirg yeht taht snilboG ym egrahc ,eoG
With dry Convultions, shorten vp their sinewes
sewenis rieht pv netrohs ,snoitluvnoC yrd htiW
With aged Cramps, & more pinch-spotted make them,
,meht ekam dettops-hcnip erom & ,spmarC dega htiW
Then Pard, or Cat o' Mountaine
eniatnuoM 'o taC ro ,draP nehT


   Ari. Harke, they rore
eror yeht ,ekraH .irA   


   Pro. Let them be hunted soundly: At this houre
eruoh siht tA :yldnuos detnuh eb meht teL .orP   
Lies at my mercy all mine enemies:
:seimene enim lla ycrem ym ta seiL
Shortly shall all my labours end, and thou
uoht dna ,dne sruobal ym lla llahs yltrohS
Shalt haue the ayre at freedome: for a little
elttil a rof :emodeerf ta erya eht euah tlahS
Follow, and doe me seruice.
.eciures em eod dna ,wolloF

.tnuexE




Actus quintus: Scoena Prima.
.amirP aneocS :sutniuq sutcA


Enter Prospero (in his Magicke robes) and Ariel.
.leirA dna )sebor ekcigaM sih ni( orepsorP retnE


  Pro. Now do's my Proiect gather to a head:
:daeh a ot rehtag tceiorP ym s'od woN .orP  
My charmes cracke not: my Spirits obey, and Time
emiT dna ,yebo stiripS ym :ton ekcarc semrahc yM
Goes vpright with his carriage: how's the day?
?yad eht s'woh :egairrac sih htiw thgirpv seoG


  Ar. On the sixt hower, at which time, my Lord
droL ym ,emit hcihw ta ,rewoh txis eht nO .rA  
You said our worke should cease
esaec dluohs ekrow ruo dias uoY


   Pro. I did say so,
,os yas did I .orP   
When first I rais'd the Tempest: say my Spirit,
,tiripS ym yas :tsepmeT eht d'siar I tsrif nehW
How fares the King, and's followers?
?srewollof s'dna ,gniK eht seraf woH


  Ar. Confin'd together
rehtegot d'nifnoC .rA  
In the same fashion, as you gaue in charge,
,egrahc ni euag uoy sa ,noihsaf emas eht nI
Iust as you left them; all prisoners Sir
riS srenosirp lla ;meht tfel uoy sa tsuI

,lleC ruoy sdnef-rehtaew hcihw euorg-eniL eht nI

,gniK ehT :esaeler ruoy llit egduob tonnac yehT

,detcartsid eerht lla ediba ,sruoy dna ,rehtorB siH

,meht reuo gninruom redniamer eht dnA
Brim full of sorrow, and dismay: but chiefly
ylfeihc tub :yamsid dna ,worros fo lluf mirB
Him that you term'd Sir, the good old Lord Gonzallo,
,ollaznoG droL dlo doog eht ,riS d'mret uoy taht miH
His teares runs downe his beard like winters drops
spord sretniw ekil draeb sih enwod snur seraet siH
From eaues of reeds: your charm so strongly works 'em
me' skrow ylgnorts os mrahc ruoy :sdeer fo seuae morF
That if you now beheld them, your affections
snoitceffa ruoy ,meht dleheb won uoy fi tahT
Would become tender
rednet emoceb dluoW


   Pro. Dost thou thinke so, Spirit?
?tiripS ,os ekniht uoht tsoD .orP   


  Ar. Mine would, Sir, were I humane
enamuh I erew ,riS ,dluow eniM .rA  


   Pro. And mine shall.
.llahs enim dnA .orP   
Hast thou (which art but aire) a touch, a feeling
gnileef a ,hcuot a )eria tub tra hcihw( uoht tsaH
Of their afflictions, and shall not my selfe,
,efles ym ton llahs dna ,snoitcilffa rieht fO
One of their kinde, that rellish all as sharpely,
,yleprahs sa lla hsiller taht ,ednik rieht fo enO

?tra uoht neht d'uom reildnik eb ,yeht sa noissaP
Thogh with their high wrongs I am strook to th' quick,
,kciuq 'ht ot koorts ma I sgnorw hgih rieht htiw hgohT

eiruf ym tsniag ,nosaer relbon ym htiw ,teY

secarg yht yap lliw I ;ts'wollof uoht mih oT
Home both in word, and deede: Most cruelly
ylleurc tsoM :edeed dna ,drow ni htob emoH

:rethguad ym dna ,em esv ,osnolA uoht diD

,tcA eht ni rerehtruf a saw rehtorb yhT

,duolb dna ,hselF .naitsabeS won t'rof d'hcnip tra uohT

naitsabeS htiw ,mohw ,erutan dna ,esromer dllepxE

,eeht euigrof od I :gniK ruoy d'llik euah ereeh dluoW

gnidnatsrednv riehT :tra uoht hguoht llarutannV

edit gnihcorppa eht dna ,llews ot snigeB

erohs elbanosaer eht llif yltrohs lliW

meht fo eno ton :yddum dna ,eluof yl won tahT

,lleC ym ni reipaR dna ,taH eht em hcteF

tneserp efles ym dna ,em esacsid lliw I

,tiripS ylkciuq :enialliM emitemos saw I sA

.eerf eb gnol ere tlahs uohT

.mih eritta ot spleh dna ,sgnis lleirA

,I kcus ereht ,skcus eeB eht erehW

,eil I ,lleb spilswoC a nI

eilf eod I ekcab sttaB eht nO
after Sommer merrily.
.ylirrem remmoS retfa

,won euil I llahs ,ylirrem ,ylirreM
Vnder the blossom that hangs on the Bow
woB eht no sgnah taht mossolb eht rednV


   Pro. Why that's my dainty Ariell: I shall misse
essim llahs I :lleirA ytniad ym s'taht yhW .orP

,tra uoht sa elbisiuni ,pihs sgniK eht oT

.etaeb eciwt eslup ruoy ere rO

,ydob yht ecarbme I ,eeht ot ekaeps won s'oD
And to thee, and thy Company, I bid
dib I ,ynapmoC yht dna ,eeht ot dnA
A hearty welcome
emoclew ytraeh htiw ,sdnema ednim ym fo noitcilffa 'hT
I feare a madnesse held me: this must craue
euarc tsum siht :em dleh essendam a eraef I
(And if this be at all) a most strange story.
.yrots egnarts tsom a )lla ta eb siht fi dnA(
Thy Dukedome I resigne, and doe entreat
taertne eod dna ,engiser I emodekuD yhT
Thou pardon me my wrongs: But how shold Prospero
orepsorP dlohs woh tuB :sgnorw ym em nodrap uohT
Be liuing, and be heere?
?ereeh eb dna ,gniuil eB


  Pro. First, noble Frend,
,dnerF elbon ,tsriF .orP  
Let me embrace thine age, whose honor cannot
tonnac ronoh esohw ,ega eniht ecarbme em teL
Be measur'd, or confin'd
d'nifnoc ro ,d'rusaem eB


   Gonz. Whether this be,
,eb siht rehtehW .znoG   
Or be not, I'le not sweare
eraews ton el'I ,ton eb rO


   Pro. You doe yet taste
etsat tey eod uoY .orP   
Some subtleties o'th' Isle, that will nor let you
uoy tel ron lliw taht ,elsI 'ht'o seiteltbus emoS
Beleeue things certaine: Wellcome, my friends all,
,lla sdneirf ym ,emoclleW :eniatrec sgniht eueeleB
But you, my brace of Lords, were I so minded
dednim os I erew ,sdroL fo ecarb ym ,uoy tuB
I heere could plucke his Highnesse frowne vpon you
uoy nopv enworf essenhgiH sih ekculp dluoc ereeh I
And iustifie you Traitors: at this time
emit siht ta :srotiarT uoy eifitsui dnA
I will tell no tales
selat on llet lliw I


   Seb. The Diuell speakes in him:
:mih ni sekaeps lleuiD ehT .beS   


  Pro. No:
:oN .orP  
For you (most wicked Sir) whom to call brother
rehtorb llac ot mohw )riS dekciw tsom( uoy roF
Would euen infect my mouth, I do forgiue
euigrof od I ,htuom ym tcefni neue dluoW
Thy rankest fault; all of them: and require
eriuqer dna :meht fo lla ;tluaf tseknar yhT
My Dukedome of thee, which, perforce I know
wonk I ecrofrep ,hcihw ,eeht fo emodekuD yM
Thou must restore
erotser tsum uohT


   Alo. If thou beest Prospero
orepsorP tseeb uoht fI .olA   
Giue vs particulars of thy preseruation,
,noitaureserp yht fo sralucitrap sv euiG
How thou hast met vs heere, whom three howres since
ecnis serwoh eerht mohw ,ereeh sv tem tsah uoht woH
Were wrackt vpon this shore? where I haue lost
tsol euah I erehw ?erohs siht nopv tkcarw ereW
(How sharp the point of this remembrance is)
)si ecnarbmemer siht fo tniop eht prahs woH(
My deere sonne Ferdinand
dnanidreF ennos ereed yM


   Pro. I am woe for't, Sir
riS ,t'rof eow ma I .orP   


   Alo. Irreparable is the losse, and patience
ecneitap dna ,essol eht si elbaraperrI .olA   
Saies, it is past her cure
eruc reh tsap si ti ,seiaS




   Pro. I rather thinke
ekniht rehtar I .orP   
You haue not sought her helpe, of whose soft grace
ecarg tfos esohw fo ,epleh reh thguos ton euah uoY
For the like losse, I haue her soueraigne aid,
,dia engiareuos reh euah I ,essol ekil eht roF
And rest my selfe content
tnetnoc efles ym tser dnA


   Alo. You the like losse?
?essol ekil eht uoY .olA   


  Pro. As great to me, as late, and supportable
elbatroppus dna ,etal sa ,em ot taerg sA .orP  
To make the deere losse, haue I meanes much weaker
rekaew hcum senaem I euah ,essol ereed eht ekam oT
Then you may call to comfort you; for I
I rof ;uoy trofmoc ot llac yam uoy nehT
Haue lost my daughter
rethguad ym tsol euaH


   Alo. A daughter?
?rethguad A .olA   
Oh heauens, that they were liuing both in Naples
selpaN ni htob gniuil erew yeht taht ,sneuaeh hO
The King and Queene there, that they were, I wish
hsiw I ,erew yeht taht ,ereht eneeuQ dna gniK ehT
My selfe were mudded in that oozie bed
deb eizoo taht ni deddum erew efles yM
Where my sonne lies: when did you lose your daughter?
?rethguad ruoy esol uoy did nehw :seil ennos ym erehW


  Pro. In this last Tempest. I perceiue these Lords
sdroL eseht euiecrep I .tsepmeT tsal siht nI .orP  
At this encounter doe so much admire,
,erimda hcum os eod retnuocne siht tA
That they deuoure their reason, and scarce thinke
ekniht ecracs dna ,nosaer rieht eruoued yeht tahT
Their eies doe offices of Truth: Their words
sdrow riehT :hturT fo seciffo eodA


   Alo. Where thou bee'st he or no,
,on ro eh ts'eeb uoht erehW .olA   
Or some inchanted triflle to abuse me,
,em esuba ot ellfirt detnahcni emos rO

esluP yht :wonk ton I )eneeb euah I etal sA(

,eeht was I ecnis dna :doolb dna ,hself fo sa staeB
Th' affliction of my minde amends, with which
hcihw htiw ,sdnema ednim ym fo noitcilffa 'hT

Here Prospero discouers Ferdinand and Miranda, playing at
ta gniyalp ,adnariM dna dnanidreF sreuocsid orepsorP ereH
Chesse.
.essehC


  Mir. Sweet Lord, you play me false
eslaf em yalp uoy ,droL teewS .riM  


   Fer. No my dearest loue,
,euol tseraed ym oN .reF   
I would not for the world
dlrow eht rof ton dluow I


   Mir. Yes, for a score of Kingdomes, you should wrangle,
,elgnarw dluohs uoy ,semodgniK fo erocs a rof ,seY .riM   
And I would call it faire play
yalp eriaf ti llac dluow I dnA


   Alo. If this proue
euorp siht fI .olA   
A vision of the Island, one deere Sonne
ennoS ereed eno ,dnalsI eht fo noisiv A
Shall I twice loose
esool eciwt I llahS


   Seb. A most high miracle
elcarim hgih tsom A .beS   


   Fer. Though the Seas threaten they are mercifull,
,lluficrem era yeht netaerht saeS eht hguohT .reF   
I haue curs'd them without cause
esuac tuohtiw meht d'sruc euah I


   Alo. Now all the blessings
sgnisselb eht lla woN .olA   
Of a glad father, compasse thee about:
:tuoba eeht essapmoc ,rehtaf dalg a fO
Arise, and say how thou cam'st heere
ereeh ts'mac uoht woh yas dna ,esirA


   Mir. O wonder!
!rednow O .riM   
How many goodly creatures are there heere?
?ereeh ereht era serutaerc yldoog ynam woH
How beauteous mankinde is? O braue new world
dlrow wen euarb O ?si edniknam suoetuaeb woH
That has such people in't
t'ni elpoep hcus sah tahT


   Pro. 'Tis new to thee
eeht ot wen siT' .orP   


   Alo. What is this Maid, with whom thou was't at play?
?yalp ta t'saw uoht mohw htiw ,diaM siht si tahW .olA   
Your eld'st acquaintance cannot be three houres:
:seruoh eerht eb tonnac ecnatniauqca ts'dle ruoY
Is she the goddesse that hath seuer'd vs,
,sv d'reues htah taht esseddog eht ehs sI
And brought vs thus together?
?rehtegot suht sv thguorb dnA


  Fer. Sir, she is mortall;
;llatrom si ehs ,riS .reF  
But by immortall prouidence, she's mine;
;enim s'ehs ,ecnediuorp llatrommi yb tuB
I chose her when I could not aske my Father
rehtaF ym eksa ton dluoc I nehw reh esohc I
For his aduise: nor thought I had one: She
ehS :eno dah I thguoht ron :esiuda sih roF
Is daughter to this famous Duke of Millaine,
,enialliM fo ekuD suomaf siht ot rethguad sI
Of whom, so often I haue heard renowne,
,enwoner draeh euah I netfo os ,mohw fO
But neuer saw before: of whom I haue
euah I mohw fo :erofeb was reuen tuB
Receiu'd a second life; and second Father
rehtaF dnoces dna ;efil dnoces a d'uieceR
This Lady makes him to me
em ot mih sekam ydaL sihT


   Alo. I am hers.
.sreh ma I .olA   
But O, how odly will it sound, that I
I taht ,dnuos ti lliw yldo woh ,O tuB
Must aske my childe forgiuenesse?

   Alo. I say Amen, Gonzallo
ollaznoG ,nemA yas I .olA   


   Gon. Was Millaine thrust from Millaine, that his Issue
eussI sih taht ,enialliM morf tsurht enialliM saW .noG

Beyond a common ioy, and set it downe

Where he himselfe was lost: Prospero, his Dukedome
emodekuD sih ,orepsorP :tsol saw eflesmih eh erehW
In a poore Isle: and all of vs, our selues,
,seules ruo ,sv fo lla dna :elsI eroop a nI
When no man was his owne
enwo sih saw nam on nehW


   Alo. Giue me your hands:
:sdnah ruoy em euiG .olA   
Let griefe and sorrow still embrace his heart,
,traeh sih ecarbme llits worros dna efeirg teL
That doth not wish you ioy
yoi uoy hsiw ton htod tahT


   Gon. Be it so, Amen.
.nemA ,os ti eB .noG   


Enter Ariell, with the Master and Boatswaine amazedly following.
.gniwollof yldezama eniawstaoB dna retsaM eht htiw ,lleirA retnE


O looke Sir, looke Sir, here is more of vs:
:sv fo erom si ereh ,riS ekool ,riS ekool O
I prophesi'd, if a Gallowes were on Land
dnaL no erew sewollaG a fi ,d'isehporp I
This fellow could not drowne: Now blasphemy,
,ymehpsalb woN :enword ton dluoc wollef sihT
That swear'st Grace ore-boord, not an oath on shore,
,erohs no htao na ton ,droob-ero ecarG ts'raews tahT
Hast thou no mouth by land?
?dnal yb htuom on uoht tsaH
What is the newes?
?sewen eht si tahW

EPILOGVE, spoken by Prospero.
.orepsorP yb nekops ,EVGOLIPE


Now my Charmes are all ore-throwne,
,enworht-ero lla era semrahC ym woN
And what strength I haue's mine owne.
.enwo enim s'euah I htgnerts tahw dnA
Which is most faint: now 'tis true
eurt sit' won :tniaf tsom si hcihW
I must be heere confinde by you,
,uoy yb ednifnoc ereeh eb tsum I
Or sent to Naples, Let me not
ton em teL ,selpaN ot tnes rO
Since I haue my Dukedome got,
,tog emodekuD ym euah I ecniS
And pardon'd the deceiuer, dwell
llewd ,reuieced eht d'nodrap dnA
In this bare Island, by your Spell,
,llepS ruoy yb ,dnalsI erab siht nI
But release me from my bands
sdnab ym morf em esaeler tuB
With the helpe of your good hands:
:sdnah doog ruoy fo epleh eht htiW
Gentle breath of yours, my Sailes
seliaS ym ,sruoy fo htaerb eltneG
Must fill, or else my proiect failes,
,seliaf tceiorp ym esle ro ,llif tsuM
Which was to please: Now I want
tnaw I woN :esaelp ot saw hcihW
Spirits to enforce: Art to inchant,
,tnahcni ot trA :ecrofne ot stiripS
And my ending is despaire,
,eriapsed si gnidne ym dnA
Vnlesse I be relieu'd by praier
reiarp yb d'ueiler eb I esselnV
Which pierces so, that it assaults
stluassa ti taht ,os secreip hcihW
Mercy it selfe, and frees all faults.
.stluaf lla seerf dna ,efles ti ycreM
As you from crimes would pardon'd be,
,eb d'nodrap dluow semirc morf uoy sA
Let your Indulgence set me free.
.eerf em tes ecnegludnI ruoy teL

FINIS. THE TEMPEST.
.TSEPMET EHT .SINIF
gnihT siht ,enwo dna ,wonk tsuM
Acknowledge mine
enim egdelwonkcA


   Cal. I shall be pincht to death
htaed ot thcnip eb llahs I .laC   


   Alo. Is not this Stephano, my drunken Butler?
?reltuB neknurd ym ,onahpetS siht ton sI .olA   


  Seb. He is drunke now;
;won eknurd si eH .beS  
Where had he wine?
?eniw eh dah erehW


  Alo. And Trinculo is reeling ripe: where should they
yeht dluohs erehw :epir gnileer si olucnirT dnA .olA  
Finde this grand Liquor that hath gilded 'em?
?me' dedlig htah taht rouqiL dnarg siht edniF
How cam'st thou in this pickle?
?elkcip siht ni uoht ts'mac woH


  Tri. I haue bin in such a pickle since I saw you last,
,tsal uoy was I ecnis elkcip a hcus ni nib euah I .irT  
That I feare me will neuer out of my bones:
:senob ym fo tuo reuen lliw em eraef I tahT
I shall not feare fly-blowing
gniwolb-ylf eraef ton llahs I


   Seb. Why how now Stephano?
?onahpetS won woh yhW .beS   


  Ste. O touch me not, I am not Stephano, but a Cramp
pmarC a tub ,onahpetS ton ma I ,ton em hcuot O .etS  


   Pro. You'ld be King o'the Isle, Sirha?
?ahriS ,elsI eht'o gniK eb dl'uoY .orP   


  Ste. I should haue bin a sore one then
neht eno eros a nib euah dluohs I .etS  


   Alo. This is a strange thing as ere I look'd on
no d'kool I ere sa gniht egnarts a si sihT .olA   


   Pro. He is as disproportion'd in his Manners
srennaM sih ni d'noitroporpsid sa si eH .orP   
As in his shape: Goe Sirha, to my Cell,
,lleC ym ot ,ahriS eoG :epahs sih ni sA
Take with you your Companions: as you looke
ekool uoy sa :snoinapmoC ruoy uoy htiw ekaT
To haue my pardon, trim it handsomely
ylemosdnah ti mirt ,nodrap ym euah oT


   Cal. I that I will: and Ile be wise hereafter,
,retfaereh esiw eb elI dna :lliw I taht I .laC   
And seeke for grace: what a thrice double Asse
essA elbuod ecirht a tahw :ecarg rof ekees dnA
Was I to take this drunkard for a god?
?dog a rof draknurd siht ekat ot I saW
And worship this dull foole?
?eloof llud siht pihsrow dnA


  Pro. Goe to, away
yawa ,ot eoG .orP  


   Alo. Hence, and bestow your luggage where you found it
ti dnuof uoy erehw egaggul ruoy wotseb dna ,ecneH .olA   


   Seb. Or stole it rather
rehtar ti elots rO .beS   


   Pro. Sir, I inuite your Highnesse, and your traine
eniart ruoy dna ,essenhgiH ruoy etiuni I ,riS .orP   
To my poore Cell: where you shall take your rest
tser ruoy ekat llahs uoy erehw :lleC eroop ym oT
For this one night, which part of it, Ile waste
etsaw elI ,ti fo trap hcihw ,thgin eno siht roF
With such discourse, as I not doubt, shall make it
ti ekam llahs ,tbuod ton I sa ,esruocsid hcus htiW
Goe quicke away: The story of my life,
,efil ym fo yrots ehT :yawa ekciuq eoG
And the particular accidents, gon by
yb nog ,stnedicca ralucitrap eht dnA
Since I came to this Isle: And in the morne
enrom eht ni dnA :elsI siht ot emac I ecniS
I'le bring you to your ship, and so to Naples,
,selpaN ot os dna ,pihs ruoy ot uoy gnirb el'I
Where I haue hope to see the nuptiall
llaitpun eht ees ot epoh euah I erehW
Of these our deere-belou'd, solemnized,
,dezinmelos ,d'uoleb-ereed ruo eseht fO
And thence retire me to my Millaine, where
erehw ,enialliM ym ot em eriter ecneht dnA
Euery third thought shall be my graue
euarg ym eb llahs thguoht driht yreuE


   Alo. I long
gnol I .olA   
To heare the story of your life; which must
tsum hcihw ;efil ruoy fo yrots eht eraeh oT
Take the eare strangely
ylegnarts erae eht ekaT


   Pro. I'le deliuer all,
,lla reuiled el'I .orP   
And promise you calme Seas, auspicious gales,
,selag suoicipsua ,saeS emlac uoy esimorp dnA
And saile, so expeditious, that shall catch
hctac llahs taht ,suoitidepxe os ,elias dnA
Your Royall fleete farre off: My Ariel; chicke
ekcihc ;leirA yM :ffo erraf eteelf llayoR ruoY
That is thy charge: Then to the Elements
stnemelE eht ot nehT :egrahc yht si tahT
Be free, and fare thou well: please you draw neere.
.ereen ward uoy esaelp :llew uoht eraf dna ,eerf eB


Exeunt. omnes.
.senmo .tnuexE




EPILOGVE, spoken by Prospero.
.orepsorP yb nekops ,EVGOLIPE


Now my Charmes are all ore-throwne,
,enworht-ero lla era semrahC ym woN
And what strength I haue's mine owne.
.enwo enim s'euah I htgnerts tahw dnA
Which is most faint: now 'tis true
eurt sit' won :tniaf tsom si hcihW
I must be heere confinde by you,
,uoy yb ednifnoc ereeh eb tsum I
Or sent to Naples, Let me not
ton em teL ,selpaN ot tnes rO
Since I haue my Dukedome got,
,tog emodekuD ym euah I ecniS
And pardon'd the deceiuer, dwell
llewd ,reuieced eht d'nodrap dnA
In this bare Island, by your Spell,
,llepS ruoy yb ,dnalsI erab siht nI
But release me from my bands
sdnab ym morf em esaeler tuB
With the helpe of your good hands:
:sdnah doog ruoy fo epleh eht htiW
Gentle breath of yours, my Sailes
seliaS ym ,sruoy fo htaerb eltneG
Must fill, or else my proiect failes,
,seliaf tceiorp ym esle ro ,llif tsuM
Which was to please: Now I want
tnaw I woN :esaelp ot saw hcihW
Spirits to enforce: Art to inchant,
,tnahcni ot trA :ecrofne ot stiripS
And my ending is despaire,
,eriapsed si gnidne ym dnA
Vnlesse I be relieu'd by praier
reiarp yb d'ueiler eb I esselnV
Which pierces so, that it assaults
stluassa ti taht ,os secreip hcihW
Mercy it selfe, and frees all faults.
.stluaf lla seerf dna ,efles ti ycreM
As you from crimes would pardon'd be,
,eb d'nodrap dluow semirc morf uoy sA
Let your Indulgence set me free.
.eerf em tes ecnegludnI ruoy teL
